Rumor of Telephone Conversation Between British and French Leaders; Discussing the Mediterranean Situation; Both Britain and France Deny

Berlin, [Date]: The German News Agency recently issued the following report, revealing the content of a telephone conversation between the British and French prime ministers. It is said that French Prime Minister Reynaud spoke with British Prime Minister Chamberlain at 10:10 pm on April 30 (Western European time). After discussing economic issues, Reynaud told Chamberlain, "General Weygand has fully prepared for the actions that both sides agreed on May 15, but said that Chamberlain cannot absolutely insist on the date, because such actions may have to be launched slightly later." Chamberlain seemed unhappy when he heard this and replied, "I have the impression that the people there think that time is absolutely necessary." Reynaud said, "There are still various difficulties that must be resolved with Turkey before action can be taken." Chamberlain then urged him to talk to Turkey again. Reynaud then said that he would try his best to remove "spiritual difficulties." Chamberlain then sternly demanded that Reynaud notify Britain of the preparations by May 20. After the two sides exchanged pleasantries, the telephone conversation ended at 10:25 pm (Haitong News Agency, 7th).

Paris, [Date]: German newspapers all carried news that British Prime Minister Chamberlain had a telephone conversation with French Prime Minister Reynaud on April 30 from 10:10 pm to 10:25 pm to discuss the actions that the two countries should take in the Mediterranean. The French government recently issued a communique denying this, saying that the British and French prime ministers never had such a conversation, and that the German propaganda trick is not worth mentioning (Havas, 7th).

London, [Date]: Regarding the rumors from the German side that Prime Minister Chamberlain of the British Prime Minister had a telephone conversation with French Prime Minister Reynaud on April 30, British officials, following the French authorities, firmly denied this, saying that the Prime Minister had fully exchanged views with Prime Minister Reynaud at the British-French Supreme Military Joint Conference on April 28 and that there was no need to do so again (Havas, 7th).

Fires of War Spread Across Southeastern Europe: Public in Panic and Uneasy; Rumors of German Troops Massing on Hungarian Border Awaiting Orders; Southern Nations Augmenting Military Preparations, Maintaining Vigilance; Berlin Intensifies Psychological Warfare

Basel, Switzerland - A Berlin correspondent for the *Basler Nachrichten* recently wired that Germany is again engaging in "psychological warfare," claiming it will launch an offensive on the Western Front. However, the country is accustomed to using misdirection, and it typically makes such pronouncements before taking action elsewhere. In recent days, this tactic has become even more pronounced, particularly with the fabrication of a long-distance phone call between British Prime Minister Chamberlain and French Premier Reynaud. It is believed that the intention is to create an atmosphere of disorder and unease. Notably, German propaganda has made no mention of Hungary, maintains a rather reserved attitude towards Romania, and considers Bulgaria the focal point of the European crisis, even more so than Yugoslavia and Greece. All these points are worthy of attention. (Havas, 7th)

Berlin - The main issue discussed in German newspapers today remains the rapid advance of German forces in Norway and the Anglo-French conspiracies in the Balkans. The *Berliner Börsen-Zeitung* prominently published the content of Chamberlain and Reynaud's telephone conversation (April 30th), arguing that it demonstrated the aggressive intentions of Britain and France. The premiers' talk only confirmed the military preparations of Britain and France in the Mediterranean and their intention to stir up trouble in the region. The newspaper concluded that all preparations must be completed by May 20th at the latest, at which point southeastern Europe may be engulfed in flames. (Haitong, 7th)

London - The Information Ministry stated that in the past 36 hours, German radio and news agencies have spread absurd rumors about border disputes erupting in the Balkan Peninsula. These rumors are largely contradictory, and others, originating from Berlin, were denied by Berlin itself within only one or two hours. The German purpose is clear: to disseminate false information to create an atmosphere of unease that benefits German objectives. (Reuters, 7th)

London - According to reliable sources, German troops are concentrating on the Hungarian border. Simultaneously, rumors are circulating that relations between Hungary and the Slovak state have once again become strained. Political figures here believe that Germany is about to intervene in Hungary, hoping to expand the war to the Balkan Peninsula, thereby forcing Italy to take a clearer stance. Furthermore, according to some reports, the Hlinka Guard of the Slovak People's Party has repeatedly staged demonstrations in recent weeks, following orders from the German authorities, demanding that Hungary return the land obtained under the Vienna Arbitration Award to the Slovak state. The Hungarian government is quite uneasy. In short, Hungary is in a perilous situation and may no longer be able to rely on Italy as a protector. (Havas, 6th)

Yugoslavia - German "tourists" have been arriving in Yugoslavia in a steady stream recently. Some districts have even had branch leaders of the Nazi Party assigned to them. Foreign observers here believe that Yugoslavia is likely to become the next Norway. However, unlike Norway, Yugoslavia is well-prepared militarily. The government and people of the city-state are deeply aware of the impending crisis, and therefore have been swift in preparing and maintaining vigilance. Regarding the Yugoslav army, a prominent American journalist even called it "one of the most elite armies in Europe." Germany must take this into consideration. Germany's primary goal is to exploit the 500,000 ethnic Germans within Yugoslavia to launch an offensive from within. Therefore, German political police have infiltrated Yugoslavia to secretly instruct these minorities. Under these circumstances, if Italy attempts to occupy the western coast of Yugoslavia via the Adriatic Sea, Germany will definitely send troops to invade the Croatian region of Yugoslavia. It is worth noting that Yugoslavia has made preparations, and Germany's plans may not easily succeed. (Havas, 6th)

Rome - The *Il Popolo d'Italia* reported last night that Turkey has amassed a large army on the Greek border, causing unrest in Bulgaria. The newspaper claimed that the concentration of Turkish troops may be related to the British naval activity in the eastern Mediterranean. (United Press, 7th)

Sofia, Bulgaria - Foreign observers here said that the German semi-official news agency, Deutsches Nachrichtenbüro, issued a report claiming that Turkey had concentrated troops on the Greek border. Diplomatic authorities in concerned countries have denied this. Germany's strategy is to spread alarming rumors to cause panic and unrest among the neutral small countries of southeastern Europe. However, this strategy has undoubtedly failed in Bulgaria, as relations between Turkey and Bulgaria are extremely friendly and are becoming increasingly close in an atmosphere of mutual trust. The reported troop movements are completely inaccurate. (Havas, 6th)

Germany Offers Assurances, Respects Swedish Neutrality; Swedish Army Chief Speaks on Radio, Vows to Fight for Independence and Freedom

Stockholm - Swedish Foreign Minister Günther recently stated that King Gustav V has exchanged letters with Hitler regarding the political situation. Sweden has repeatedly affirmed its neutrality, and Germany has given assurances of respecting Swedish neutrality. (Reuters, 7th)

Berlin - The official German news agency announced that German leader Hitler and Swedish King Gustav exchanged written opinions on the political situation in the latter half of April. This action has strengthened the complete alignment of future policies between the two countries, in accordance with the statements already announced by the German and Swedish governments. (Reuters, 7th)

Stockholm - General Ericsson, Commander-in-Chief of the Swedish Army, recently delivered a radio address, stating, "If we are forced by circumstances to resort to war, we will not hesitate to fight. Even though war may bring losses, if we continue to enjoy freedom, we will surely be able to quickly recover. Conversely, if we lose our freedom under foreign guardianship, what value will life and property have? We have recently understood that the interests of the nation are our interests. The nation can guarantee our security, but when necessary, it may require us to accept sacrifices, even sacrificing our lives. In this, we must be brave and unyielding to protect our country's freedom and independence." (Havas, 6th)

Turkish Parliament Passes Bill, Grants Broader Powers to Military Authorities

Istanbul - An Anqara dispatch states that the Turkish Parliament today passed ten bills, stipulating that in extraordinary circumstances, military authorities are granted broader powers, including requisitioning public and private property and services. (Reuters, 7th)

Netherlands on Alert, Officers' Leave Canceled

The Hague - The Government Information Service recently issued a communiqué stating that all leave, regular or temporary, has been canceled for officers and soldiers of the army, navy, and air force, as well as employees of war industries. (Havas, 7th)

Polish Destroyer Sunk in Norwegian Waters; Britain Compensates with Newly Built Warship; Stavanger Airport Bombed Again

London - According to an official announcement, the Polish destroyer "Grom," which has been working closely with the British fleet since the start of the war, was recently sunk by bombs while operating in the Norwegian Sea. One officer and 65 soldiers are missing and presumed dead. The British government is willing to compensate for the "Grom" with a new warship currently under construction, and the Polish government has accepted this offer. (Reuters, 7th)

London - The Polish destroyer "Grom" had a displacement of 2,144 tons, a speed of 3 knots per hour, and was equipped with four 4.7-inch guns, four anti-aircraft guns, and mine-laying equipment. The entire crew consisted of 80 officers and soldiers. At the beginning of the European war, it and other Polish warships joined the British fleet, under the command of the British naval authorities. (Havas, 6th)

London - It has now been learned that Captain Wynne, commander of the British destroyer "HMS Havant," which was bombed and sunk by German aircraft while escorting troop transports in Norwegian territorial waters, has been rescued and is safe. The ship's survivors departed from a port in Scotland last night, heading south. (Reuters, 7th)

Paris - The Ministry of the Navy recently announced that a British and French convoy, escorted by our warships, was attacked by German aircraft in the North Sea on the 3rd of this month. German aircraft dropped multiple bombs, but none hit the transport ships. Only our destroyer "Bison" was sunk, but most of the sailors have been rescued. (Havas, 6th)

London - It is now known that a squadron of British bombers, led by Squadron Leader Thorold, bombed the Stavanger airfield in Norway yesterday, temporarily rendering it ineffective. Enemy anti-aircraft guns and fighter planes put up strong resistance. All but two of the British planes returned to base. It is reported that the two missing planes were last seen after the squadron reached its target, spread out, and dropped bombs individually. (Reuters, 7th)

Estimated Losses of German Merchant Ships Reach Approximately 600,000 Tons Since Outbreak of War

London - The Admiralty announced that since April 1st, the Germans have lost a total of 300,000 tons of merchant ships, most of which were sunk during the Norwegian campaign. This does not include transport ships and supply ships. The above figure brings Germany's losses since the start of the war to 600,000 tons, accounting for 15% of Germany's pre-war total tonnage. Confirmed captures, sinkings, or self-scuttling of German merchant ships total 454,000 tons. It is estimated that there are another 30 unidentified ships, totaling 150,000 tons, that have been sunk by Allied submarines, mines, and aircraft. According to reports from Rotterdam, the German motor vessel "Robert Ley" (27,288 tons) sank in the Skagerrak on the evening of April 12th. There are also reports of two German ships sinking near Delfzijl. In the week ending late on April 28th, German actions resulted in the sinking of four British ships totaling 6,689 tons, one Allied ship of 1,458 tons, and two neutral ships totaling 298 tons. The names of the above ships are not to be released under the new regulations. British losses in tonnage are less than one-third of the average weekly losses to date. The convoy system continues to be successful. As of May 1st, a total of 19,098 British, Allied, and neutral ships had been convoyed, with 31 being sunk. Meanwhile, 3,457 ships were convoyed by the French, with 7 being sunk. Although the Germans have heavily bombed our ships in Norwegian territorial waters, our ships have put up extremely strong defenses. One ship was attacked more than forty times in a single day, with German aircraft dropping 150 bombs, none of which hit. There were no casualties on board. The ship's anti-aircraft guns shot down two enemy aircraft and damaged four others. Another warship escorting troop transports shot down five enemy aircraft in three days. As far as is known, there are currently no German ships in Narvik or Norwegian territorial waters north of there. (Reuters, 7th)

Gold Mine Discovered in Soviet Union

Moscow - Soviet geologists have recently discovered seven gold deposits in Komsomolsk. (TASS, 7th)

US Focuses on Far East, Pacific Fleet to Remain; Public and Government Sympathize with China, Condemn Illegal Aggression; Broad Embargo Against Japan Under Discussion in Congress

Washington - Naval experts here declared yesterday that although the European war is raging, the United States is still focusing its attention on the Far East. This spring's large-scale maneuvers by the US fleet in the Pacific demonstrate America's concern for the Far East more clearly than any official statement. After the exercises, the US fleet will remain indefinitely in several locations in the Pacific. Because the Latin and British countries neighboring the Pacific mutually abolish armaments based on friendly relations, the only meaning of the US fleet concentrating in the Pacific is to prevent difficulties in the Far East. The fact that the US Navy does not prepare for defense on the American Atlantic coast shows America's bias towards Asia. This defense surprises the Europeans, who are fighting each other to the death, but this fact can be explained by a part of the general American belief. America's views on Europe: first, it recognizes that the powers of Europe are roughly equal to each other, and no country seems to threaten American security; second, the legendary West (the West refers to Asia) is the border of the United States and where American commercial interests lie; third, in the Far East, Japan's naval and military forces are very powerful, while China and the Soviet Union may experience disturbances, and their preparations are relatively limited. In comparison, the forces are quite uneven, and any incident is likely to occur; fourth, the United States has territories on the islands in the Pacific, which must be guaranteed security. The relationship between the United States and any Far Eastern country is based on the hope of stabilizing the status quo in the Pacific and expanding trade. The official and non-official sympathy of the United States towards China stems from the American belief that China, which is moving towards a modern national economy and modern politics, should be allowed to develop itself and should not be interfered with by other countries. Therefore, in the past, the United States opposed Russia's aggression against China, and now, it at least diplomatically resists Japan's aggression against China. The basic requirement of the US policy towards China is the Nine-Power Treaty of 1922. This provision stipulates that any country should respect the territorial and administrative integrity of China and should not take any action to monopolize China's economic interests. The United States opposes Japan's establishment of puppet governments in Manchuria and Central China. The United States only recognizes the Chongqing government, which is at war with Japan, as the legitimate government of China. In order to increase the Chongqing government's ability to resist the war, the United States has indirectly lent China US$45,000,000 and has repeatedly warned Japan diplomatically to encourage China's resistance. Japan has now become the most detested object of the United States. The United States has repeatedly protested Japan's occupation of Chinese territory, denouncing it as illegal and endangering American rights in China. Some of these rights are guaranteed by the US-Japan Treaty. US-Japan relations are now very tense, so the United States has taken the step of abolishing the US-Japan Commercial Treaty. Although at present only a moral embargo is adopted in terms of gasoline and aircraft exports, several broader embargoes against Japan are under discussion in Congress, but no decision has been made. A broad embargo can be implemented with the approval of the President and the Secretary of State. However, the President and the Secretary of State must act prudently and only implement such a plan when the whole country believes that it is necessary. At this time, loans to China, moral embargoes, and certain indirect means have been adopted. For example, the United States' increased shipbuilding program is one of the indirect actions. Although this is not a direct opposition to Japan, it is obviously designed for Japan's expansionist forces. Naval officers have stated that the number of Japanese fleets is already unknown, so the United States needs to build new ships. Another naval officer also expressed his personal opinion that a US-Japan war is inevitable. Since President Roosevelt took office, the United States has completed 122 new ships, with 72 currently under construction. There are also 43 others that have been passed by Congress, and 24 have been drafted and will be sent to Congress. There are also 43 that have been passed by the House of Representatives. Recently, the most attention has been paid to the issue of the Dutch East Indies. The statement issued by Japan is generally regarded as Japan intending to take the opportunity to occupy the Dutch East Indies once Germany occupies the Netherlands. Regarding the Dutch East Indies issue, the US government has warned Japan that the United States is extremely concerned about any changes in the status quo of the Dutch East Indies. Many observers believe that the result of the Sino-Japanese War will inevitably be mutual destruction. At this time, if the Soviet Union is not very strong, the balance of power in the Far East can still be established, and the United States will be quite satisfied at this moment. The current lack of vigorous action is partly due to waiting for the outcome of the incident and partly due to the hope that once the European war ends, Britain and France will cooperate more actively with the United States in the Far East. (United Press, 7th)

Panama Canal Defenses Consolidated; US Deputy Chief of Staff Speaks, Ready to Assist All States

Washington - US Army Deputy Chief of Staff Major General Sterett, speaking recently at the American Society of Engineers, strongly stated that the Panama Canal Zone's defenses are consolidated and sufficient to cope with any eventuality. He said, "Any attempt to sabotage the Panama Canal has been considered by the authorities and measures have been taken to prevent it." The construction of the new locks will be completed in 1945, at which time defense efficiency will increase by 50%. If an aggressor is determined to obtain a base in the territory of the American republics, the defense forces of each country are weak and insufficient to cope with it. It is actually necessary for us to send troops to assist, so that foreign countries do not destroy the territorial integrity of our neighboring countries. If an invaded country obtains a base in a certain republic in the Americas, we and this republic will be threatened. Therefore, we must deploy a strong military force, ready to move at any time, so that we can quickly defeat any "blitzkrieg" attempt. (Havas, 6th)

US Naval Officers Hold Meeting, Review Recent Sea Maneuvers

Honolulu - More than 650 US naval officers, chaired by Admiral Richardson, Commander-in-Chief of the US Battle Fleet, held a meeting here yesterday to review recent sea maneuvers in the Pacific. (United Press, 7th)

Japanese Envoys' Meeting in Latin America; Kato to Attend in Brazil; Paraguayan Envoy Tours Japan

Washington - Kato, a representative of the Japanese Ministry of Foreign Affairs, recently departed from here to the capital of Brazil to attend a meeting of Japanese envoys stationed in Latin American countries to discuss various issues related to Japan's interests in each country. According to Japanese sources here, Kato will assume the post of Ambassador to Brazil. (Havas, 6th)

Kobe - An economic delegation led by former Paraguayan Senator Chirife is currently touring Japan. They recently held a meeting here with Japanese business leaders and unanimously adopted a joint declaration emphasizing the need to increase trade between Paraguay and Japan, stating that Paraguay can export agricultural and daily products to Japan, while Japan can export various industrial products to Paraguay. At the request of the Paraguayan economic delegation, the Japanese Businessmen's Association of South America has urged all parties concerned to import Paraguayan raw cotton, canned meat, agricultural products, and other products. Five Percent Rehabilitation Loan to be Repaid in July, Lottery Drawn in London

London - HSBC announced that the Chinese government's 5% Rehabilitation Gold Loan of 1913, of which £537,020 was drawn by lottery at the London head office on March 5th of this year, will be repaid in full on July 1st of this year. Interest on bonds drawn for repayment will cease immediately. (Reuters, 7th)

Norwegian Foreign Minister Koht Leaves England for France Today; Reportedly Wishes Sweden to Maintain Neutrality; Britain Refutes Claim of Imprisoning Norwegian Commander

London - Norwegian Foreign Minister Koht told a Reuters reporter yesterday that Norway had suffered heavy losses, with many casualties and missing persons. The Norwegian army had also lost a large part of its forces. However, there were still excellent Norwegian troops in the north, which were completely unharmed. This army would be of great help to the Allied forces, as it was the most elite in the Norwegian army, familiar with the rugged terrain, and well-equipped, but lacking anti-aircraft guns. There were approximately 50,000 to 100,000 German troops in Norway. In any case, their number was quite large. The Norwegian government had never sought help from Sweden, as Norway did not want its Swedish friends to suffer the same pain as the Norwegians and share the same fate. Sweden would, to the best of its ability, maintain its neutrality, but how things would evolve in the future was difficult to predict. When the reporter asked about the rumors of Norwegians such as Quisling being traitors, Koht replied that he had never heard of any Norwegian treason. There were Norwegians who sympathized with the Nazis, but there was no treason. (Reuters, 7th)

London - Foreign Minister Koht, in response to widespread rumors that the German army's invasion of Norway was aided by Norwegian collaborators, stated yesterday that this was inaccurate. He said, "We have not discovered any clear acts of treason. The German army's entry into Norway was easy due to the sudden attack. You cannot blame us for not taking precautions. The truth is that we never expected the German army to invade." Koht also denied the claim that the mines in the Oslo Fjord and other bays were sabotaged by traitors, rendering them ineffective, as there were no mines laid in those waters. (Reuters, 7th)

London - Foreign Minister Koht met with Prime Minister Chamberlain this afternoon. Afterwards, he told a Havas reporter, "I plan to travel to Paris on the 8th of this month for a two or three day stay to hold talks with French Prime Minister Reynaud, Defense Minister Daladier, and other key figures." He then met with reporters from various newspapers and stated, "In this chaotic world, our country is not isolated and helpless. Thinking of this fills me with excitement. The ideals that our country cherishes are no different from those cherished by Britain and France. We have always recognized ourselves as a small country with exceptionally weak military strength. It was difficult for us to shoulder major responsibilities in the international arena, so we strictly adhered to neutrality, not daring to overstep. Today, we have been forced into war to defend our homeland. But we ask ourselves if we have done anything to deserve this. Therefore, our determination to resist is even stronger." (Havas, 7th)

Norwegian Troops Defend the Glomma River

London - The Norwegian Telegraph Agency reported that Norwegian troops were still holding the Glomma River between Røros and Støren. 250 German soldiers crossed Røros yesterday and headed towards Glomdalsfjella. Norwegian troops in Trøndelag, northeast of Elverum, were ordered to retreat after the Allied forces withdrew. It was reported that the Germans had arrested many civilians, accusing them of aiding the Norwegian army. (Reuters, 7th)

Berlin - The German High Command announced today that German troops advancing north from South Namsos and Grong had reached Mosjøen, 180 miles northeast of Trondheim. It also claimed that a submarine chaser had sunk a submarine in the Skagerrak and that two British planes had been shot down by German fighters while attempting to fly over the Siragrun Bay. (Reuters, 7th)

Stockholm - Norwegian troops are advancing towards Mosjøen and Bodø in the hope of making contact with the British and French Allied forces fighting near Narvik. However, German troops are also advancing towards the area. (Havas, 7th)

Stockholm - An evening newspaper here recently reported that Norwegian troops were clashing with German troops between Rögnas and Singhus, with fierce fighting. Several thousand German soldiers had launched repeated attacks, but were repelled. However, large numbers of German reinforcements were still arriving at the front, one battalion of which was traveling from —Sete to Roås. (Havas, 6th)

They stated that General Ruge had voluntarily boarded the British warship, which was solely for the use of Ruge and his staff. His subsequent actions were decided by Ruge himself. Ruge is currently in Norway. (Reuters, 7th)

French Troops Retreating Arrive in Scotland

London - French expeditionary forces withdrawing from central Norway have arrived at a port in northern Scotland aboard several transport ships. Although these troops were heavily bombed by German planes during their retreat from the front lines and boarding the ships, they did not suffer a single casualty. A French battalion commander told the press after landing that they had been stationed in Norway for ten days and had not seen any German troops. However, the area where they landed was heavily bombed by German planes, causing heavy losses to the residents. There were no military targets in the area, but the German planes not only bombed but also strafed with machine guns. The residents sought refuge in the mountains, and even the Allied soldiers mostly hid in the nearby forests during the day, only coming out at night. (Havas, 6th)

Papal See in Rome Denies Rumors

It was claimed that although the Holy See and Portugal would sign a political agreement today, it was unrelated to the Swiss newspaper report. Pope Pius hoped that even if war broke out in the Mediterranean and Italy was drawn into the conflict, the Holy See would not leave the Vatican. (Haitong, 7th)

Pound Sterling Falls in New York Market; Hong Kong Dollar and French Franc Also Decline; Japanese Government Bonds Fall in Price in Britain

Central Authorities Express Determination to Maintain Currency System; Claims of Restricting Withdrawals are Pure Rumors, Firm Statement Sent to Shanghai Chamber of Commerce

Chongqing, 7th - Recently, due to seasonal financial factors, speculators have taken the opportunity to disrupt the market, causing fluctuations in the Shanghai exchange rate. The government is making every effort to maintain stability. However, malicious individuals have spread rumors that the government will further restrict withdrawals in Shanghai, causing public anxiety. Upon hearing this news, the Ministry of Finance stated that since the beginning of the war of resistance, the government has been determined to maintain currency credibility and stabilize the financial system. All financial policies are based on this principle. The above rumors were fabricated by speculators and traitors in an attempt to disrupt public morale and undermine the financial system, which is abhorrent. The Shanghai Chamber of Commerce and the Banking Association have been instructed to declare that there is no such thing. It is hoped that when this message reaches Shanghai, the rumors will be refuted on their own, demonstrating the futility of the rumor-mongers' efforts.

Banking Industry's Receipts and Payments Resume Normalcy Yesterday

Since the black market foreign exchange in Shanghai has been maintained by the Exchange Stabilization Fund Committee, the British and American exchange rates have been relaxed, the market has stabilized, rumors have gradually subsided, and public confidence has slightly improved. Yesterday, the HSBC exchange rate was the same as the day before, while the US exchange rate decreased by 0.125, which is considered stable. The run on banks and financial institutions has indeed completely subsided, and the normal state of receipts and payments has resumed since yesterday. It is reported that at the beginning of this bank run, the Central Bank of China, the Bank of China, and the Bank of Communications supplied the industry with as much cash as possible to meet the withdrawal needs of the banks and financial institutions. A reporter from the New Voice News Agency visited a financier yesterday who stated that the Shanghai environment is becoming increasingly difficult year by year, and the market has been alarmed repeatedly, especially this year. However, the banking industry has taken into account the interests of depositors, customers, society, and the government's wartime financial policies, preserving the nation's vitality, leading by example, refraining from improper business practices, and assisting the authorities in suppressing speculation.

Firm Belief in Resistance and Nation-Building; Commemorating May 7th

Yesterday was the May 7th National Humiliation Day, commemorating the day in 1915 when Japan presented China with the Twenty-One Demands, requiring a response within 48 hours. Yuan Shikai, who was seeking foreign support to establish himself as emperor, recognized the demands on May 9th. The Chinese community in the city did not hold a commemorative ceremony yesterday, but unanimously reaffirmed their determination to resist and build the nation, support the government, and strive for final victory.

Limit of 50 Yuan per person, effective this month

The limit for inland travelers carrying legal tender for export was previously set at 500 yuan, but was reduced to 200 yuan in February of this year. The Zhejiang Customs has recently received an order from the Ministry to limit each person to 50 yuan, which has been implemented this month.

Coal Dust Market Actually Uses US Dollars for Pricing; Improper Measures Alienate the People; Nanyang Coal Briquette Factory Sells Coal Briquettes at Discounted Prices

The Nanyang Coal Briquette Factory began selling coal briquettes at discounted prices yesterday, setting up ten discounted sales points, each selling 20 dan per day, totaling 200 dan per day. Sales hours are from 2:00 PM daily until sold out. Each person is limited to purchasing 3 jiao of national currency at a time, which is equivalent to 4 catties of coal briquettes, until the end of this month. The ten discounted sales points are listed below: (1) Song Taichang, 154 Route des Pères; (2) Xieyuan, 270 Rue Cardinal Mercier; (3) Dasen, 126 Rue Sazare; (4) Qiantai Xing, 202 Shanhai Pass Road; (5) Jiufeng, Lane 53, No. 66 Ximen Road; (6) Fuchang, 6 Route Grelier; (7) Kunyuan Xing, 206 Ximen Road; (8) Yixing, 985 Tokyo Road; (9) Yuxing, 220 Route Tenant de la Tour; (10) Yongmao, 68 Rue Jules Pasteau.

Priced in US Dollars

A reporter from Datong News Agency interviewed the Coal Industry Association. Mr. Qi-sheng, a member of the Standing Committee of the Association, told the reporter that the coal dust market has been pricing transactions in US dollars since May 5th, which caused him great indignation. It was found that the current price of coal dust is US$7 per ton, equivalent to RMB 155. The market price has risen, and all future transactions will be based on the US dollar. Daily necessities such as raw materials for coal briquettes are actually priced in US dollars. Even from the perspective of knowledgeable people in the industry, this is considered inappropriate.

A Glimpse of Corruption According to Mr. Bao Zhezhi, it is also a public secret that hoarders are manipulating the coal briquette market. Therefore, it is hoped that the coal industry can be cautious in selecting its customers. Orders for coal dust or coal briquettes placed by outsiders through insiders should be treated with caution, without consideration for personal relationships. People in the industry should not seek extra profits and act as accomplices. Coal briquette factories must strictly enforce the rejection of delivery orders from speculators. Raw material suppliers must not sell to third parties who are not in the coal briquette industry. Finally, it is hoped that the Public Works Department will have absolute disciplinary measures.

Notice Regarding Postal Parcels

Notice from the Parcel Section of the Postal Administration: (1) Large parcels and bulk small packages to various locations in the Fujian area will be resumed, but the weight of each parcel (except those to Xiamen) should be limited to 20 kilograms. (2) Large parcels, commercial parcels, and bulk small packages to Hengshui, Jixian, Nangong, and their surrounding areas in the Hebei area should be temporarily suspended. (3) Large parcels and bulk small packages to the Jiaozhou Bureau in the Jiangsu area can now be resumed. (4) All types of parcels and bulk small packages to Maanshan, Shushan Town, Huwen Town, Dapu, and other places in the Jiangsu area should be temporarily suspended. (5) Parcels and bulk small packages to Fanxian Bureau and Sang'azhen Agency (under the jurisdiction of Guanxian Bureau) in the Shandong area should be temporarily suspended. (6) Parcels and bulk small packages to Mengyin and Chaocheng Bureaus, as well as individual scattered parcels and medicine parcels to Gaocheng Bureau, can now be accepted as usual. (7) Individual scattered parcels and medicine parcels to Daxingzhuang in the Su area can now be resumed.

Regulations for Sending Parcels with German Goods

Same Treatment for Shipments to Germans

Notice from the Postal Administration: Parcels and small packages passing through Vietnam that contain German goods or are sent from or to German citizens will be temporarily suspended from acceptance. However, if the sender indicates on the package "to be forwarded via domestic postal routes" and the domestic postal routes are indeed passable, this restriction does not apply. This matter was previously notified in the Bureau's Notice No. 1606 on April 4 of this year. Now, it has been determined that samples passing through Vietnam that contain German goods or are sent from or to German citizens will be treated the same way.

Public Works Department Cracks Down on Prices; Emphasizes Public Reports; Yu Huaqing's Observations on Rising Prices of Daily Necessities Confirm That It Is an Excuse to Seek Illegitimate Profits Through Exchange Rates

The Shanghai Times reported that the Public Works Department of the Public Concession issued a notice on May 3rd prohibiting merchants selling essential goods from unreasonably raising prices by taking advantage of fluctuations in the legal tender exchange rate. A reporter recently asked Mr. Cabot, Deputy Director-General of the Public Works Department, who is responsible for handling this matter, about the effect of the notice. Cabot replied that no one had reported anything yet, so the Public Works Department had not taken action against those who hoard and profiteer. Three weeks ago, the Public Works Department issued a notice asking the public to report hoarding and profiteering. If the public reports, the Bureau will definitely investigate. The reporter asked if this meant that the Public Works Department would not take any action unless a report was made. Cabot replied that it was indeed the case, and that the Bureau was awaiting reports. If there was a significant case of hoarding and profiteering, a special committee would be formed to investigate.

Mr. Yu's Opinion

Due to recent fluctuations in the exchange rate, various industries have raised their selling prices, especially for daily necessities, causing great hardship to people in the middle and lower classes, and making each day seem like a year for the working class. A reporter from the New Voice News Agency visited Mr. Yu Qiaqing, a leader in the Shanghai business community, to seek his opinion. Mr. Yu granted an interview and made the following remarks. Mr. Yu said that all prices in Shanghai have soared recently, with the excuse being fluctuations in the exchange rate, but this is not actually true. Even if the exchange rate fluctuated, the first to be affected would naturally be imported goods. Calculating the fastest possible delivery time, goods would need at least three months to arrive in Shanghai to be affected by the depreciation of the exchange rate. Therefore, the goods currently sold in stores are all in stock, so there is no reason to raise prices immediately. For example, on the morning of May 2nd, when the exchange rate fluctuated, some stores immediately raised prices by 30%, which is extremely absurd. This is actually using the fluctuation of the exchange rate as an excuse to seek illegitimate profits, which is unfair. As for rice and coal briquettes, which have also risen recently, this is even more inappropriate. These two items are essential for the daily life of ordinary people and are of utmost importance.

First, let's talk about coal briquettes. Some time ago, the Chamber of Commerce invited the coal industry to repeatedly discuss fair prices. The original price of coal dust was set at 100 yuan per ton. The cost of shipping was calculated at 28 shillings per ton, resulting in a loss of about 5 shillings. Now that the cost of shipping has been reduced to 23 shillings per ton, it is exactly 100 yuan per ton, without any loss. The cost of manufacturing coal briquettes is about 15-16 yuan per ton, plus a profit of 4-5 yuan, making it 20 yuan per ton. Adding the profit of 4-5 yuan for coal shops and 1-2 yuan for transportation, the total cost is 126 yuan per ton, or 6.3 yuan per dan. Even if affected by the exchange rate, the cost of coal dust would only increase by 20 yuan, totaling 146 yuan per ton at most. How can it be as high as 190 yuan per ton? Moreover, how can the exchange rate affect goods in stock? Are all the manufacturing costs, shipping costs, and profits of coal briquettes in Shanghai also calculated in foreign exchange and raised in price accordingly? Or are they saying that there is no significant profit to be made from making coal briquettes, so they will raise the price and sell them to yarn factories instead? If this is the case, their intentions seem inappropriate. In addition, for the sake of maintaining fair prices some time ago, the Chamber of Commerce invited the coal industry to repeatedly discuss and reach an agreement. Even if there is an immediate impact on prices due to the fluctuation of the exchange rate, they should request the Chamber of Commerce to state their reasons and reconvene to discuss the matter. However, they have resolutely taken action and raised prices twice in the past few days, no wonder the citizens are comparing them to taking advantage of a disaster.

As for rice

The price has also been rising uncontrollably. Is the rice being sold in the market now the goods that have arrived after the exchange rate fluctuation? If not, is the recent price increase due to the rice merchants and general speculators manipulating and hoarding goods? Any discerning person can see this. If this continues, how will the livelihoods of ordinary people be sustained? Weighing the pros and cons, the concession authorities and the city's Chamber of Commerce must take effective measures to curb this. Shanghai has a population of 4 million. How can we sit idly by and ignore the livelihoods of the majority of people for the sake of the interests of a few? It is hoped that merchants in all industries will prioritize their conscience in this extraordinary period, so that we can overcome the difficulties together. Otherwise, the future of Shanghai is at stake. What is the use of striving for unjust wealth?

Sales Have Stagnated

It is also learned that all items have immediately increased their selling prices during this sharp decline in the black market exchange rate. Among them, the rise in coal and coal briquettes is the most rampant. In addition, such items as cloth, hardware, general miscellaneous goods, and food have also soared in price. Some stores have even removed the price tags from their goods and are raising prices arbitrarily, without any limits. In fact, due to the extremely high cost of living and the difficulty of maintaining it, consumers in Shanghai have already been trying their best to save money. Therefore, consumption has greatly decreased. The current inventory of various goods in Shanghai is very large due to the competition to hoard goods. Even the customs warehouses are filled to capacity. Although the customs have repeatedly urged the release of goods, the sales are limited, and speculators are still trying to hoard goods, so many have not been released from the warehouses. Other clothing and miscellaneous goods are also experiencing an oversupply due to reduced consumption. In the end, those who only seek profit will only have themselves to blame.

Automobile Wireless Radios Shipped to Hong Kong: Import Prohibited

Since the outbreak of the European War, the Hong Kong government has been engaged in various wartime measures. A reporter from the Da Guang News Agency learned yesterday from transportation industry sources that the Commissioner of Trade Control in Hong Kong recently issued a decree prohibiting the import of automobiles and wireless radios. This includes the engines and chassis of automobiles. Therefore, recent shipments of these items have been forced to return to Shanghai. According to the regulations, the following conditions must be met for import: (A) The consignment note must state that the goods are being shipped outside of Hong Kong. (B) The goods must be in transit or transferred from one ship to another for shipment outside of Hong Kong. (C) If the goods can be packaged, they must be packed in sturdy boxes. (D) A detailed list of the goods must be submitted to the Commissioner of Trade Control before departure. (E) If the goods are transferred from one ship to another, a detailed list of the goods must also be submitted to the Commissioner of Trade Control before departure. Fortunately, the relevant industries are paying close attention to avoid losses.

Resumption of Work at the British United Shipyards; General Wage Increase of 15%; Amendment of the Agreement; Dismissed Workers to Receive Severance Pay

More than 1,000 workers at the Great Union Shipyards (i.e., the British-owned Ruirong, Yesong, Xiangsheng, Hefeng, United Shipyards) went on strike starting on March 14th of this year due to the factory's failure to fulfill the agreement of December 6, 1939. Mediation by the Municipal Council was ineffective, resulting in a stalemate. Recently, through the efforts of Gu Bingyuan of the Industrial Section, a complete resolution has been reached. The employer has now increased wages by 15% in accordance with the original wages, continued to recognize the union's subsidy of 100 yuan per month for loyalty fees, permanently dismissed more than 40 workers, and issued severance pay. Other improvements have been amended and announced by both parties to the agreement. All workers resumed work yesterday morning.

Brief Record of the Agreement

The British United Shipyards posted the revised labor-management agreement in the form of a notice at the entrances of each factory. A summary of the agreement is as follows: (Agreement with Workers) (1) The company recognizes the right of workers to represent the permanent fitters, lathe operators, coppersmiths, pattern makers, electricians, welders, and workshop laborers in each of the company's factories. Workers who have not been employed for a full twelve months are not entitled to the benefits stipulated in this agreement. (Bonus) (2) The company will pay a bonus to workers at the end of the year, but only if the company has dividends to distribute to shareholders. The amount of the bonus shall not be less than 10% of wages or more than 15% of wages. (Dismissal) (3) The company agrees not to dismiss any worker without just cause. Just cause refers to the following items. If any of the following reasons exist, the company has the right to dismiss workers: A. Continued business downturn for the company. B. Reduction of workers due to reorganization of various workshops in the company. C. Workers' failure to obey orders. D. Workers' commission of theft or other improper conduct. E. Workers' negligence of duty. F. Workers' repeated tardiness. G. Workers' repeated or intentional violation of company rules. (Shift Work) (4) The company may transfer workers to shift work if it deems it necessary due to a business downturn, but guarantees that workers will have at least twelve days of work out of every twenty-eight days, and will continue to be paid during the shift period. However, if workers work elsewhere during the shift period, the company will not provide a subsidy. Workers on shifts must report to the company's accounting department between 9:30 AM and 11:30 AM to collect the subsidy voucher. If the unfavorable business conditions continue to extend, the company has the right to dismiss workers.

Dismissal Allowance

If dismissal must be implemented, the company shall pay a dismissal allowance, the amount of which is as follows: Those who have worked for one year or more but less than three years will receive 25 days' wages. Those who have worked for three years or more but less than five years will receive 35 days' wages. Those who have worked for 30 years or more but less than 40 years will receive 125 days' wages. The company shall give two weeks' notice if it wishes to dismiss a worker, but this method shall be subject to the circumstances at the time. (Holidays) (5) Annual holidays are set at ten days. (Accident and Injury Allowance) (6) If a worker is injured while performing his duties, the company shall pay for medical expenses and continue to pay his wages and subsidies for three months during the treatment period. If the worker has not recovered after three months or becomes permanently disabled, the company shall provide compensation and severance pay based on the worker's years of service, with a maximum amount of 350 yuan. If a worker dies or dies from serious injuries due to an accident while performing his duties, the nearest relative will receive a pension, with a maximum amount of 450 yuan. If a worker dies within two months due to an accident while performing his duties, in addition to medical expenses, the company shall continue to pay wages and subsidies until the date of death and provide a pension, with a maximum amount of 450 yuan.

Various Prohibitions

(Illness and Death Benefits) (Omitted) (Work Stoppage or Strike) (9) If workers are dissatisfied, they shall notify the company of the reasons and shall notify the company of the reasons 48 hours in advance. They shall not stop work without authorization. Those who strike without permission shall automatically lose the rights stipulated in this agreement. Those who intentionally damage company property or use violence to prevent others from working shall be dismissed by the company and have their due rights canceled. If a strike by one worker affects the work of other non-striking workers, the company shall not be responsible for the wages lost by those who cannot work as a result. In the event of an illegal strike, the company has the right to lock all workers out of the factory. (Subsidy) The company agrees to continue to pay all workers a subsidy of two yuan per week (six or seven working days) as the standard, based on the Shanghai Municipal Council's survey of the average weekly price of No. 1 local white rice at 30 to 40 yuan per dan, for a period of one year. (Unauthorized Posting) (10) (13) Workers agree not to post or write in chalk any notices or advertisements within the company or on any part of the company's property without the permission of the factory authorities. Violations of this clause shall be treated as a violation of company rules in accordance with Clause 3. If a worker is found to have violated this chapter, he shall be subject to dismissal. (Workers' Requests) (14) When workers have legitimate requests, they shall be submitted to the company by the official workers' representatives who signed the agreement. The company does not recognize any interference from outside organizations. If there is a change in workers' representatives, the company shall be notified immediately and the signatures of the new representatives shall be submitted to the company and attached to this agreement. (Mediation) (15) If mediation is required for the application of any of the items in this agreement, both parties agree to jointly invite the Mediation Office to handle it. (Effective Date of Agreement) (16) This agreement shall take effect from the date of signature and shall be valid for two years, except as otherwise provided in Article 12. All previously agreed labor-management contracts shall be abolished. (Interpretation of English and Chinese Agreement) (10) (17) In the event of any discrepancy in the interpretation of the Chinese and English texts of this agreement, the English text shall prevail.

Hundreds of White Russian Youths in "Manchukuo" to Come to Shanghai; "Manchukuo" to Compel White Russians to Serve in the Military; Those Unwilling Plan to Flee to Shanghai

According to the Continental News, Changchun officially announced last month that starting from January 1, 1941, all White Russian youths in "Manchukuo" must serve in compulsory military service and join the "North Manchurian Army." Therefore, it is expected that several hundred White Russians from Harbin and other cities in "Manchukuo" will flee military service and move to Shanghai this year. It is reported that the "Manchukuo" conscription law was first promulgated last year, but it was implemented on a small scale, and due to the lack of military instructors, most White Russian youths were not forced to enlist. However, the number of military instructors has recently increased, and a new order was issued last month stating that starting next year, the conscription law will be applied to all White Russian youths in "Manchukuo," and large-scale military education for White Russian youths will begin. According to White Russians who came to Shanghai from Harbin, most White Russians in that area plan to come to Shanghai. The White Russian population in this city was about 25,000 two years ago and has now increased to 50,000.

Lin Yutang's Remarks in the Philippines: America Believes China Will Win; If America Imposes an Embargo, Japan Will Be Placed in a Desperate Situation; Chinese People United as Never Before

Americans are Confident that China Will Win

All Conspiracies Have Failed

The Japanese are currently trying to consolidate the Chinese territories they have occupied, but they have also failed. Remittance Exchange Premiums Greatly Stabilized

Profiteers Lose Their Basis

After August 13th, remittances could not be used to purchase foreign exchange, and the scope of transfers was limited to the financial industry in China. Among merchants, some gradually reduced the remittance of business income by one or two yuan per hundred yuan to obtain legal tender for their needs. Afterwards, the number of remittances on the market increased, and the amount of cash felt to be insufficient in return. As a result, those who collected legal tender to buy remittances for profit seized the opportunity to rise up. The exchange premium market soared. Since the Central Bank, Bank of China, and Bank of Communications commissioned banks to jointly adjust the legal tender needs of the money industry, the exchange premium market price has been greatly stabilized. However, since remittances can be converted into cash, as time goes by, more and more people are taking advantage of this, and the blockade of funds has thus had loopholes. The money industry's supply to customers is inherently limited to the genuine needs of importers, but it is impossible to be as strict as expected in reality. Since July 1st of last year, after the new system of strengthening remittances, the preparation committee's supply of cash withdrawals for remittances from various industries was stopped at the same time. Although speculators were still able to profit from the market slump at first, and forcibly held on, now that the commercial beliefs of the citizens have gradually recovered, and various industries have recognized the importance of fund blocking, the new remittance system is becoming more and more strengthened. The new remittances have been well received by industry and commerce. Foreign banks have already begun to accept the new remittances. The remittance payment reserve is now based on more than 100% of assets, so there will be no soaring market prices like those that occurred in April of last year, and speculators are gradually losing their base.

Patrolman Loses His Mind, Shoots Driver and Passengers; Quarrel Over Prolonged Traffic Light Time; Patrolman Became Enraged and Opened Fire Indiscriminately; Four People Were Shot; The Patrolman Abandoned His Post and Fled

At approximately 11:20 AM yesterday, a shooting incident occurred at the intersection of Avenue Edward VII and Gordon Road in the Public Concession involving a patrolman and a tram driver. As a result, two tram passengers were shot, one person was startled and fell, and the tram driver was also shot in the head and seriously injured. The patrolman lost his mind, opened fire indiscriminately for a moment, like a madman. Seeing the disaster he had caused, he abandoned his gun, took off his uniform, and fled without a trace. The details are as follows:

Patrolman Obstructs

At approximately 11:00 AM yesterday, a tram on Route 1, driven by driver No. 119, was traveling east from Jing'an Temple. When it passed the intersection of Gordon Road and Avenue Edward VII, the patrolman No. 2618, who was in charge of the traffic lights, did not turn on the green light for a long time, causing the tram to be unable to move forward. At that time, the driver, He Dengshan (26 years old, from Nantong), believed that the tram had a company-regulated time schedule for each run, so he was very dissatisfied and spoke rudely. The patrolman was also young and hot-tempered, so he stepped forward and angrily slapped He's face. The matter was resolved after passengers and passersby persuaded them to stop.

Opening Fire Indiscriminately

At approximately 11:20 AM, when the tram returned to the intersection of Gordon Road and Avenue Edward VII from the Bund, the two first glared at each other, and then a quarrel broke out. The patrolman tried to drag He out of the tram, and He angrily said, "Dare you shoot me?" Before he could finish speaking, the patrolman ignored the consequences and pulled out his gun, firing four shots at He and the front of the tram. Amid the sound of gunfire, He was the first to be hit, and a bullet hit his head. At the same time, two passengers standing on the platform, Hu Mingyi (18 years old, from Jiangxi Jiang) and Wu Liangen (also known as Liquan, 22 years old), were also hit. Hu was shot in the chest, and Wu was shot in the right shoulder, both collapsing in a pool of blood. In addition, an old man, Ye Xuanji (63 years old, from Wujin), was too frightened and fell out of the tram, breaking his leg.

Abandoning His Post and Fleeing

For a moment, passersby did not understand the truth and thought that there was a robbery and the police were shooting, so they rushed to avoid the scene, causing great confusion. The Chinese patrolman who committed the crime saw the disaster he had caused, quickly took off his uniform, and escaped without a trace while the opportunity presented itself. Afterwards, the police received the news and sent officers to the scene to transport the injured to the Bao Long Hospital for treatment. They also launched a strict search for the patrolman. It is reported that the police found the gun that the patrolman had been carrying in a trash can somewhere on Tianzhu Road within an hour after the incident.

Also Affected Was the Old Accountant of Yuan Heng Trading Company

Loss of 4,500 Yuan

The Kidnapping Case of Feng and Li Remains Unresolved to This Day

Definitely a Mistaken Kidnapping Since They Are Not Wealthy

The kidnapping case of Feng Yunjii, director of the tobacco leaf department, and Li Zhitang, director of the cigarette packaging department, of the Nanyang Brothers Tobacco Company, which occurred on Yu Yuan Road the day before yesterday (the 2nd), remains unresolved to this day. Reporters visited their families separately. According to them, Feng and Li have both been working at the Nanyang Brothers Tobacco Company for many years, working hard and diligently. They have been promoted from small employees earning 30 yuan a month to the position of director. However, their position in the company is only that of middle-level employees, and their monthly income is only enough to feed their families. Feng and Li are colleagues with equal positions, and their family situations are about the same. It is difficult to guess what the purpose of the kidnapping is. Since the two men are not wealthy and usually focus on company business and do not ask about other external affairs, it is certain that this kidnapping was a mistaken kidnapping.

Nationally Produced Seasoning with a Certified Seal of Authenticity

Seasoning powder is a necessity for daily use. However, some manufacturers of seasoning powder often cut corners, produce inferior goods, or even change labels to deceive the people, which is harmful to health. This is no small matter. The Shanghai National Seasoning Powder Manufacturers Association has specially obtained approval from the Ministry of Economic Affairs to print national product certification seals. Starting from March 1st, these seals will be distributed to member factories to be affixed to each product. In addition to the Ministry's order to overseas embassies and consulates, as well as domestic customs offices and anti-smuggling agencies, to conduct strict inspections, the association will also conduct thorough inspections and detailed chemical tests. Any products that do not meet the standard ingredients will not be allowed to be released, in order to maintain the reputation of national seasoning products. Those unscrupulous people who impersonate national products will have no way to use their skills from now on.

The association's planning prices were: 24 crude white, this warehouse goods were 76.7 yuan, foreign warehouse new goods were 76.7-76.5 yuan, old goods were 76.3-76.2 yuan, transshipment goods were 60 yuan, Taikoo car white B mark 487 yuan, and the large ones were 86.5 yuan, which can be obtained. This warehouse was 66.7 yuan, transshipment was 55.5 yuan, H mark car red was 63 yuan, and the rest lacked changes. 300 foreign packages of Guotang Diao Qing were transacted yesterday, and the price was 62-62.7 yuan, which was 5 yuan higher than the previous (2nd). Dozens of pieces of Tiao Qing were still 52 yuan. It was heard that Xinghua Qing was 470 yuan, but it was too far away.

North and South Goods: Golden Daylily Also Subject to Control, How Can Market Prices Be Cheap?

Golden daylilies have always been traded through remittance and transfer. Recently, the premium has exceeded 200 yuan outside the customs. Although it has slightly recovered recently, the source is still subject to control by a certain market, so external expenses have increased sharply, and the cost is even higher. Currently, sales have also become active, and the trend is quite strong. According to production news, this year's new goods must be marked at 50 yuan, so everyone is unanimously optimistic. It is reported that a batch of Guangbang's top-grade vegetables was 55 yuan the day before, and even the prices of regular goods have risen sharply in recent days. It is estimated that more than 70 bags from Zhongxing Suqian were 48 yuan, Daxing vegetables were 52 yuan, and Gaoxiangzhuang was 53.5 yuan. It is said that the price will increase by 10 yuan before and after.

Silk and Tea: New Tea Market Opening

In the past two days, the new green tea produced and sold by foreign firms, the manufacturers have put one or twenty new samples on the market. Yesterday, more than one hundred boxes of fine tea leaves were collected by Xiehe, Shihe, Jinlong and other firms, with prices ranging from 430 yuan to 460 yuan. According to the cost estimate of the merchants, all of them will inevitably suffer losses, and the situation is slightly unprofitable. It is reported that most of the new and old goods recently purchased by various firms are for export on the Italian postal ship "Contro Rosso". At this time of the Mediterranean war, both Chinese and foreign tea merchants are mostly taking a wait-and-see attitude.

Education News

China Education and Culture Foundation, Awards and Subsidies for Science Graduate Students, 35 Selected in the 28th Year

(Hong Kong Correspondence) The Board of Directors of the China Education and Culture Foundation, awards and subsidizes scientific research. The personnel who have received scientific research awards and subsidies in the 28th year are as follows:

(1) Winners of Scientific Research Awards: Xu Xifan, research on parasitology, received 2,000 national currency;

(2) Winners of Scientific Research Subsidies: (A) Continued Subsidies, (I) Overseas Subsidies: Lin Shi'e and Liu Yi Jin, both studying aeronautical engineering in the United States; Wang Yunzhang studying agronomy in the United States; Shen Qingnang, Zhang Quan, and Chen Shenzhao, all studying chemistry in the United States; Cheng Chongdao studying chemistry in Germany; Wang Dezhao studying physics in France; Wang Pu studying physics in the United States; Zhang Jiawei studying soil science in the United States; He Zuolin studying geology in Germany; Chang Lin Ding studying zoology in France; the above subsidies are all US$800 each; (II) Special Subsidies: Zhang Jingquan studying chemistry at a domestic university, and Shen Jiarui studying zoology, each received 500 national currency; (B) Newly Granted Subsidies, (I) US Subsidies (Designated Subjects): Gu Peimu on aviation engines, Sun Shouquan on ore dressing, Xie Jialan on steel, Ma Zhuzhen on non-ferrous metals, Li Qingyuan and Xu Keqin on economic geology, Huang Tie on veterinary medicine, Sun Yunpei on insecticides, Xiao Zhidi on fisheries, Liu Bingyang on microbiology; the above are all studying in the United States, and the subsidies are all US$800 each; (II) Domestic Subsidies: Chen Dai on ceramics and Ding Hanbo on zoology, each receiving 1,000 national currency; (III) Special Subsidies: Zheng Ji, Lin Guo Hao, and Li Liang, all researching chemistry; Wu Xiang and Li Chun You, both researching physiology; Wu Guang on parasitology; Lin Changshan on entomology; Liu Xianren on agronomy; the above each received 500 national currency.

Second Anniversary of the Death of Musician Huang Zi Wu

Memorial Ceremony Held in the Provisional Capital

(Chongqing, 7th Telegram) The 9th is the second anniversary of the death of musician Mr. Huang Ziwu. Ceremonies will be held throughout the country on this day, and his posthumous works will be played. The music circles of the Provisional Capital will hold a memorial ceremony on this day in the auditorium of the Music Cadre Training Class of the Central Training Corps. At 7 o'clock in the evening, famous artists will separately broadcast Mr. Huang's representative works to China and the United States.

A Letter to All Shanghai Students from the University and Middle School Student Association

(Three)

Second, we must use the program of resistance and national reconstruction as our goal of hard struggle.

Reading is of course our basic work, but our hard struggle must also have a definite goal. Otherwise, we will easily be tempted and shaken, and there will be the danger of blindly following others. We know that China's only way out now is to resist to the end. Of course, we oppose any peace compromise. However, long-term resistance is indeed a very difficult and arduous task. Because the purpose of this resistance is not only to resist Japanese aggression. We are not only engaged in resistance, but also actively engaged in national reconstruction, establishing a new country of freedom and equality. Therefore, resistance and national reconstruction are progressing simultaneously. To achieve the goal of winning the resistance and succeeding in national reconstruction, the first thing we must do is strengthen our self-esteem and self-confidence. Young people are the pillars of the country, and we should especially strengthen our

belief in resistance.

Leading the people to participate in the work of resistance and national reconstruction. However, as I said before, studying hard is saving the country. This means that we students must engage in saving the country through our basic work. In other words, we must do appropriate extracurricular activities. We must be a model for the people and hold an absolutely optimistic attitude towards the country. We must clearly recognize our goal: the purpose of long-term resistance is to build a new China of independence, freedom, and the Three Principles of the People. Compromise along the way is suicide. Therefore, we oppose the deceptive peace of surrender to the people. We must eliminate the small number of wavering elements in our ranks. Of course, we also hope that they will have a final awakening and be able to abandon evil and return to righteousness and participate in the work of resistance and national reconstruction together. We must clearly recognize that this resistance is the

only way

for the Chinese nation to strive for independence, freedom, and equality. The responsibility of saving the country must be shouldered by everyone. This time, Chairman Chiang Kai-shek also made it clear to us at the Fifth National Political Council, "No matter how difficult the environment of resistance has been in the past two years, the national policy of resistance has always been firm." The reason why the national policy of resistance can be so firm is because the people of the whole country have consistently supported the program of resistance and national reconstruction. We students have the most glorious history in the past, so when it comes to such a great festival, we cannot but encourage each other. Most importantly, we must clearly judge right and wrong and distinguish between good and evil.

Provincial Zhenzhong Subject Competition

Jiangsu Provincial Zhenjiang Middle School, since the start of this semester, has maintained a stable environment, and students are also able to concentrate on their studies. It is said that the principals and teachers employed by the school, such as Ye Shaonong, Zhu Tingmao, Yao Yixiang, Li Tianmin, Shi Ze, Chen Qinan, Wu Juchen, Lu Songshi, Wu Zhengwei, Qian Sufan, etc., are all diligently working hard and teaching conscientiously. Currently, in order to encourage students' interest in learning, the school is holding various subject competitions. Last week, a calligraphy competition was held. The results were: first place in large characters, Tang Guangtao; second place, Leng Yinde; third place, Ren Yueqin. First place in small characters, Zhu Liangju; second place, Wang Taili; third place, Tang Guangtao. This week, essay competitions will be held. The high school essay topic is "On the Necessity of Building Oneself Before Building the Nation," and the junior high school essay topic is "How to Be a Good Student."

Sports News

The 10th Public Exhibition Handball Championship Already in the Grasp of Zhongqing; Three Doubles Matches Won Last Night; Tonight's Outcome is Irrelevant

After the tenth Public Exhibition Cup handball competition, with both the Chinese and Western sides each winning one round, the final decisive round has resulted in a difficult-to-resolve balanced situation. The acquisition or loss of the championship therefore depended on the five doubles matches that began last night. The Zhongqing side, recognizing the seriousness of the situation and the need to deploy unconventional tactics in order to win, decided to bring up Jiang Jiadu and Sun Jialu from the student ranks and replace Gao Zisan of the fifth group and Cheng Zunhua of the third group. Their strength has thus become even more formidable. Zhongqing is determined to win. In last night's three matches, apart from the extremely tense situation in the fourth group, the fifth and third groups won with overwhelming momentum, each winning in straight sets. Currently, Zhongqing has won the third round with an 8-5 victory. In the overall results, they have triumphed with a 2-1 victory. The championship is already within their grasp. There are still two main group battles tonight, but the outcome is irrelevant.

Wangdu Participates in Grass Court League

A Total of Nine Teams in Group A

The Curtain Rises on the Tenth of Next Month

The registration for this year's Group A and B league, organized by the Shanghai Grass Court Tennis Association, closed a few days ago. Nine teams are participating in Group A and ten teams in Group B. Group A has one more team than last year. In addition to the eight old members, there is also the newly emerging Chinese powerhouse, the Wangdu Tennis Club. It has been two years since Chinese players gave up participating in this competition. The sudden rise of Wangdu will surely rival the China Tennis Club and Kangdi Tennis Club, which previously dominated the competition. Group B has one less team than last year. The old members, the German team and the Waterworks team, have withdrawn. The Jewish Club has joined as a new team. The Group A competition is scheduled to begin on the 19th of next month, and the Group B competition will begin earlier, on the 5th of next month. The team lists are recorded below.

Group A: British American Tobacco, French Chamber of Commerce, Portuguese Chamber of Commerce, Citibank, Xiejiao Club, Wangdu, North Grass Court, South Grass Court, Japanese Club.

Group B: French Club, French Chamber of Commerce, Portuguese Chamber of Commerce, Japanese Club, Jewish Club, Western Police A, Western Police B, North Grass Court, South Grass Court, Swiss Club.

Police Sports Two-Mile Race, Nine Teams Participate in the Competition

The Hongkou Cross-Country Team Hopes for the Championship The工部局 (Gong Bu Ju) police officers' spring sports meet will be held on the 25th of this month. There are a total of fifteen Chinese and Western teams participating in the two-mile open team championship. Chinese teams account for as many as nine. The Hongkou Cross-Country Team A group is the strongest and is quite confident in winning this year's championship. In order to prepare for winning the championship, the entire Hongkou team is scheduled to hold a general test run this weekend (12th) at 6:30 AM in Jiaozhou Park. The lineups of its A, B, and C teams are as follows:

(A) Wang Zhenglin, Guan Youwen, Wang Shiying, Wan Jinsheng; (B Team) Gu Qiming, Zhou Ruquan, Le Kangyi, Yang Linfa; (C Team) Huang Cangguan, Ni Weida, Wu Jingde, Wang Yakin.

Jingwu Cup Ping Pong Match, Chuan Qifang Wins

In the Jingwu Cup table tennis tournament, the fifth round was held the night before last. In the first group, Ouyang Wei defeated Guo Jingren 3-1, maintaining his winning record. Veteran Li Zongpei lost to newcomer Chuan Qifang 1-3. Chuan has recently defeated many famous players and is in the spotlight. In the third and fourth groups, Zhang Ying and Lu Hanjun defeated Pan Rixi and Huang Zhijun, respectively. Zhang and Lu were slightly superior, but under the desperate efforts of their opponents, victory did not come easily. Tonight, due to Huang Fenzhi's withdrawal, there will only be three matches.

Newspaper Clipping 67 Years Ago (377)

From the original newspaper of the 12th year of Tongzhi, Qing Dynasty

Spring Welcoming Ritual (2)

The Spring Official is usually played by a beggar, as no one is willing to take on this arduous task. The Mang God previously had a pair of glass lamp fixtures, followed by several pairs of lamp fixtures with gold characters on blue gauze. Behind him were dozens of people from various government offices, beating gongs and drums with loud shouts. Finally, incense smoke swirled around, with people carrying incense burners and incense trays walking in unison. At the very end was a gilded vermilion lacquer shrine, representing the arrival of Tai Sui. In front of the shrine were three or four layers of candle stands, filled with burning candles. The candles that had burned in front of the god were known as "yuanbao" (silver ingots) in the vernacular, and people competed to buy large candles to take home, calling it "great luck." Those who were unable to buy candles in time would throw money, either dozens, hundreds, or thousands of coins, towards the god before taking a candle away. The shopkeepers they passed would distribute leftover candles, calling it "sending yuanbao," the price of which was several times the value of the candle. Among the officials welcoming spring, the first was the director of education from the prefectural government. From the flags and gongs to the umbrellas and fans, and even the execution tools and divination sticks, all were equipped with red and black hats, and more than a dozen people held whips to clear the way. The clerks of the departments and those carrying registers and seals all wore neat attire and rode slowly past on horseback. At the end was a tiger-skin armchair, carried high by four people, representing the official seat of the prefectural governor. Next was the Water Conservancy prefectural governor, followed by the Chief Constable prefectural governor, their ceremonies similar to the first. After the three prefectural governors, the magistrates of Ren and Qian counties followed closely. The clerks and servants in the county offices were numerous, and their bright ceremonial guards were especially impressive.

Becoming a Person of the World (4)

Similarly, a certain wealthy person may be a good family head and neighbor at home, but as soon as he arrives at the office, his attitude changes drastically, becoming as cunning as a fox and as fierce as a tiger. Therefore, all those who compete with him call him an "unscrupulous person." Is he really without conscience? His conscience is only private, not public. Again, legislators, using the convenience of their positions, enact all kinds of laws that benefit the locality, without considering the interests of the entire country. People like this all need a broad conscience that puts the country first. However, nationalism, if taken to extremes, is narrow, such as illegally invading other countries, which is not a blessing for the country or the world. Therefore, they must go a step further and have a conscience for the world, regardless of language, ethnicity, or national boundaries, and seek happiness for all mankind. (3) A kind of world work, everyone should work. But why work? For life? No. If only for life, cows and horses are better at it. For the family? No, if only for the family, tigers and wolves are also good at protecting their own kind. For the country? No, if it is only for the country, how is it different from the Greeks who do not believe in Christ? The ideal of Christians is that people must work for humanity—the world. He must live in such a way that his daily work is connected with the work of promoting world evolution. He is a person with a mission, and his mission is to feed, heal, educate, and redeem the world. In ancient times, those who worked for humanity included Abraham Lincoln in the United States, who advocated the emancipation of slaves, and Wesley Livingston, who preached abroad; General Gordon, who was chivalrous and sacrificed his life for other countries. There are countless others; they are all people who worked for world humanity. In short, who is the one who has these three qualities? It is Jesus of Galilee. He devoted his life to the needs of mankind, to the transformation of the world, and sacrificed his life. He is a good model for us to be human. Finished.
